100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">大家好，我是阳子。我从英国约克大学儿童教育专业硕士毕业后，从事儿童早期教育已经有 8 个年头了。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">我是国内顶尖高校早教基地的负责人，研发的课程被上千家早教机构和幼儿园采用，帮助了超过 10 万个家庭，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">也是 2 个孩子的妈妈。</strong></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6666666666666666\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1620\" style=\"box-sizing: src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/FIBFp81yz61jG15WQIWFxzwrsO2qLbibEGQcq9UdZZBdvsnG6PPTe3zfYYRrFU9iaq4upc3LcSkPKU3vAV7TJjDw/640\"></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在从事早教行业的这么多年里，我遇到过很多家长，他们总是抱着疑虑问我：</p><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"padding-left: 13px;display: inline-block;width: 531.75px;vertical-align: top;border-left: 3px solid rgba(128, 110, 255, 0.5);border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"color: rgba(84, 84, 84, 0.6);line-height: 1.6;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">阳子老师，到底要不要给孩子做早教？</p></section></section></section><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在回答这个问题之前，我想先跟大家理清早教的概念。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">很多家长觉得做早教就是上早教班，是为了让孩子变得更聪明，或者觉得早教就是随便在网上找些游戏玩。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这些都是家长对早教常见的误区。真正的早教是在了解孩子的生长发育情况后，做一些可以对孩子产生正面影响的行为。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">所以关于要不要做早教，我的回答是，不仅要做，而且是越早开始越好。</strong><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">那早教到底对孩子有什么实质性的帮助，以及我们到底该如何给孩子做早教呢？今天就来跟大家分享下。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><section style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;\"><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: 15px;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 30px;vertical-align: middle;height: auto;align-self: center;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.7623457\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"324\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/FIBFp81yz61jG15WQIWFxzwrsO2qLbibE4VX8jqJyPDVJe8ssopOtIiaADcz4nGv23o5jwhqwPH70aXUXdXtlvxQ/640\"></section></section></section></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: 5px;margin-left: 0%;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-bottom: -6px;line-height: 1;padding-right: 5px;padding-left: 5px;font-size: 18px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">为什么要给孩子做早教？</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 100%;height: 10px;background-color: rgba(128, 110, 255, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section></section><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">婴幼儿时期是孩子大脑神经系统发育最快，也是各种感官和体能发展最为关键的时期。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">早教的意义，就是为孩子提供丰富良好的成长环境，促进孩子能力发展，一定程度上也能够提高孩子自信心。</strong><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">就举一个我身边的案例吧。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">我们早教园所曾经有一个 2 岁左右的小男孩，他在个别字母发音上有些不清晰，比如说「p」这个音他就发不出来，总是会把「婆婆」念成「波波」。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">孩子的父母一开始很着急，会让孩子反复去念那个音做矫正。但孩子总也说不太好，甚至开始有点抵触，他们就觉得要不还是顺其自然吧，等孩子长大一些，发音自然会改善。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">其实，这 2 种做法都不太可取。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">强行矫正可能会形成负面强化，让孩子更加丧失信心；</strong><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">自然发育能够让孩子说话变好一些，但却无法彻底改善。</strong><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">那我们当时是怎么解决的呢？<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">我们并没有给他做特殊的训练，只是每天设置了 10～15 分钟的「呼吸训练」，比如吹羽毛、把乒乓球吹进杯子里等小游戏。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">就这样在一个月内，每天额外花十来分钟时间，小男孩的发音就得到了彻底纠正。像这样的「呼吸训练」小游戏，<strong>可以在宝宝不抵触的情况下，帮助孩子获得语言能力的提升。</strong><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在我给丁香妈妈设计的早教课里，在语言发展区块游戏里也用了不少「呼吸训练」的方法。比如我会让孩子去吹动轨道内的乒乓球。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img class=\"rich_pages __bg_gif\" data-ratio=\"0.566\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"500\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/FIBFp81yz61jG15WQIWFxzwrsO2qLbibE4Hp1aJvI4hmSBzgtMaUuVACHicgCofHL1iaSOYFHYXwNUG7WKZOzDgicg/640\"></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;text-align: center;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <span style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(206, 206, 206);font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>图片来源：丁香妈妈《早教全攻略》课程</span></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">为什么这样就能锻炼孩子的语言能力呢？<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">因为正确控制呼吸之间的气流，是发音的基础。</strong><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">呼吸训练能够锻炼孩子的口唇肌舌肌能力，反复训练可以帮助孩子吐字更清晰。</strong><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><section style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;\"><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: 15px;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 30px;vertical-align: middle;height: auto;align-self: center;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.7623457\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"324\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/FIBFp81yz61jG15WQIWFxzwrsO2qLbibE4VX8jqJyPDVJe8ssopOtIiaADcz4nGv23o5jwhqwPH70aXUXdXtlvxQ/640\"></section></section></section></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: 5px;margin-left: 0%;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">我们该如何给孩子做早教？</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 100%;height: 10px;background-color: rgba(128, 110, 255, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: 5px;margin-left: 0%;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-bottom: -6px;line-height: 1;padding-right: 5px;padding-left: 5px;font-size: 18px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section></section></section></section><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">很多家长既是图轻松省事，也是觉得给孩子花的钱越多效果越好，喜欢把孩子送到早教班，每个星期上一两节课。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">但我们要知道，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">一般孩子的专注力时长，大概是年龄乘以系数 3</strong><strong>。</strong>比如 1 岁左右的孩子可以专注 3 分钟，2 岁的可以专注 6 分钟。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">而早教班大都是一对多的教学模式，老师很难把控每个孩子的专注情况。在 45～60 分钟的早教课上，孩子玩几分钟就跑神了，能够学到的自然微乎其微。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">那我们要如何尽可能提升孩子的专注力呢？<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">孩子更需要的一对一的关注和引导。</strong><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在拍摄丁香妈妈早教课程的时候，我们请到了一个 2 岁多的孩子。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">本来这个年龄段的孩子，可以专注 6 分钟，但这个孩子在拍摄现场完全坐不住。助教老师拿出吸管道具的时候，她非常不屑一顾。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">但老师仍然很有耐心，她通过手工设计，用吸管和黏土做出了一个小刺猬。这时候小女孩的注意力就完全被吸引了，也开始加入游戏，进行拿放的动作。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img class=\"rich_pages __bg_gif\" data-ratio=\"0.5658307210031348\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"638\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" border-box;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.4px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong>在花大量时间鼓励、引导孩子去做游戏上，父母是比早教班老师更有优势的。</strong>对孩子最好的教育，也一定是父母的陪伴和言传身教。<br style=\"max-width: sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word><strong>因此面对不同宝宝，也需要专属的早教计划。</strong></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, rgb(128, 110, 255);\"><strong>一套专业测评</strong></span>，就能为自己的宝宝定制为期 3 年的早教计划了<span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;\">。</span></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;min-height: 大维度评估宝宝的发育情况。</span></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif 0.4px;\">曾经接触过 2 个家长的案例，因为照着某线上游戏视频做早教，结果孩子从瑜伽球上摔下来受到运动伤害。</span></p><p style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica border-box;\">朱笑婕老师也是三个孩子的妈妈，刚开始她也是无比茫然，在慢慢捕捉到孩子的需求信号后，她发现，带娃其实并没有那么难。</p></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"135编辑器\"><p style=\"white-space: 10px;padding-left: 10px;line-height: 1.9;color: #545454;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">S.L.O.W 策略是育儿大师特蕾西提出的，这个单词组合起来的意思就是<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">「慢下来」</strong>。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><section data-role=\"list\"><ul class=\"list-paddingleft-2\" style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><li><p><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: #6a57ef;box-sizing: border-box;\">S（Stop）</span></strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.7px;\">：</span><strong style=\"letter-spacing: 0.7px;box-sizing: border-box;\">停下来。</strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.7px;\">先做个深呼吸让自己平静下来。</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.7px;\">哭声是宝宝的语言，不要一听到宝宝的哭闹就焦虑不已。</span></p></li></ul></section></section></section></section><section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"135编辑器\"><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0.7px;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;line-height: 1.9;color: #545454;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section data-role=\"list\"><ul class=\"list-paddingleft-2\" style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><li><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: #6a57ef;box-sizing: border-box;\">L（Listen）</span></strong>：<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">听一听。</strong>给自己时间分辨一下哭声到底是否有不同。当然，不是放任宝宝哭泣，而是暂缓行动。</p></li></ul></section><section data-role=\"list\"><ul class=\"list-paddingleft-2\" style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><li><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: #6a57ef;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">O（Observe）</strong></span>：<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">观察</strong>宝宝的肢体语言，查看周围的环境。</p></li></ul></section><section data-role=\"list\"><ul class=\"list-paddingleft-2\" style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><li><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: #6a57ef;box-sizing: border-box;\">W（What’s up）</span></strong>：综合之前三步的所见所闻<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">做出判断并回应宝宝。</strong></p></li></ul></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"135编辑器\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"135编辑器\"><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0.7px;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;line-height: 1.9;color: #545454;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">当宝宝刚来到这个世界的时候，他们与外界唯一的沟通方式只有<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: #6a57ef;box-sizing: border-box;\">哭声和肢体语言（姿态、面部表情、动作）</span></strong>，这就是他们向家长传递需求的「线索」。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">如果家长处于特别慌乱焦虑的状态下，很难抓住这些稍纵即逝的线索。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">SLOW 这个「慢」策略正好能帮助我们做出恰当的判断和行动，更有针对性地满足宝宝的需求。</p></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"135编辑器\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: #6a57ef;box-sizing: border-box;\">每 1～2 小时</span></strong>就主动去观察宝宝是否出现饥饿信号。</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">除新生宝宝、出现猛涨期的宝宝外，其余阶段的宝宝观察时间可以拉长到<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: #6a57ef;box-sizing: border-box;\"> 3～4 小时</span></strong>。</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">如果早期的饥饿信号没有被捕捉到，宝宝就会表现出一些晚期非常饥饿的信号，比如<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">很激动地扭动身体或大声哭闹</strong>。这时衔乳会比较困难，家长需要先安抚宝宝，等他平静些之后，再给他进食。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></li></ul></section><section data-role=\"list\"><ul class=\"list-paddingleft-2\" style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><li><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.7px;box-sizing: border-box;\">打挺、把头转开</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></li></ul></section><section data-role=\"list\"><ul border-box;\">推开食物、开始扔食物和勺子</span></p></li></ul></section></section></section></section><section style=\"color: #545454;letter-spacing: 0.7px;line-height: 1.9;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 做怪相</span></p></li></ul></section><section data-role=\"list\"><ul class=\"list-paddingleft-2\" style=\"padding-left: 30px;\"><li><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span
